MTA Wiki
RoutesCorridorsProjects

project

East Side Access

project_annual-2021-east-side-access

Overview

East Side Access was the MTA C&D project to bring Long Island Rail Road service into Grand Central Terminal. The 2021 annual report lists it among MTA C&D's major expansion projects, and a July 2023 capital update says ESA was "now known as Grand Central Madison (GCM)," providing direct LIRR service through an 11.5-mile underground tunnel with a new station and concourse below the existing terminal. [annual_report_narrative_2021#p094_c0004] [meeting_doc_115231#p011_c0008]

Funding And 2021 Status

As of December 2021, MTA reported $10.2 billion committed to ESA out of an $11.133 billion project budget, plus a $463 million rolling-stock reserve, with $2.699 billion of federal funding and more than $6.7 billion in third-party construction executed. The same report said ESA executed about $203.7 million of construction in 2021 and forecast public revenue service for December 2022. [annual_report_narrative_2021#p088_c0003] Reported 2021 work included Harold Structures B/C Approach, GCT Station Caverns and Track, GCT Concourse and Facilities Fit-Out, systems contracts, Mid-Day Storage Yard, passenger-experience/retail enhancements, Harold catenary work, and Eastbound Reroute. [annual_report_narrative_2021#p088_c0003] [annual_report_narrative_2021#p089_c0001]

An October 2024 capital-program amendment later described most Network Expansion work as complete and identified $463 million of remaining ESA rolling-stock reserves for a future LIRR M9A growth fleet, with the overall Network Expansion budget unchanged at $5.861 billion. [meeting_doc_155616#p019_c0004]

Service And Readiness Context

In November 2022, committee minutes still framed opening as near-term: a public commenter said an FRA waiver would allow ESA to open on schedule, while MTA C&D described C&D and LIRR as working toward GCM opening that year. [meeting_doc_102686#p002_c0005] [meeting_doc_102686#p009_c0005] MTA C&D also said GCM would increase LIRR peak service by 40% and off-peak service by 65%, and described the facility as a 700,000-square-foot terminal station with a 3.5-mile tunnel to Queens. [meeting_doc_102686#p009_c0005] [meeting_doc_102686#p009_c0006] Readiness work extended beyond the Manhattan terminal: the Great Neck Pocket Track was described as an ESA readiness project for train storage and operating flexibility supporting GCM service. [meeting_doc_102686#p004_c0005]

April 2023 timetable-change materials still listed East Side Access as a continuing project supported during the May 22 to September 5 schedule period. [meeting_doc_109341#p001_c0004] [meeting_doc_109341#p001_c0005]

Revenue Service And Closeout

By July 2023, capital-program materials said revenue service began January 25, 2023, the project was approximately 96% complete, and GCM had entered closeout. [meeting_doc_115231#p011_c0009] [meeting_doc_115231#p011_c0010] The same update says the Biltmore Connection opened May 8, 2023, linking GCM with Grand Central Terminal and a direct 43rd Street exit, while closeout work focused on test documentation, as-builts, warranties, claim resolution, and safety/security certification packages. [meeting_doc_115231#p011_c0011] [meeting_doc_115231#p012_c0003]

Later Contract Items

Post-service materials show remaining project and contract cleanup rather than a simple "done" state. In May 2023, Board materials requested a CM030 passenger-experience and finish-detailing extension to November 22, 2023 with $3,358,260 in impact costs because delayed project-system access affected the contractor; the scope included lighting, ceiling, architectural, retail, customer-information, wayfinding, and systems-integration work. [meeting_doc_112036#p029_c0007] [meeting_doc_112036#p029_c0008] [meeting_doc_112036#p029_c0009] In July 2024, Board materials requested a CS179 modification to replace fire standpipe valves in ESA tunnels and retest the fire-suppression system; the contract table listed a $1,905,486 request and $766,118,869 current amount. [meeting_doc_147196#p017_c0008] [meeting_doc_147196#p018_c0006] [meeting_doc_147196#p018_c0008]

Caveats

The December 2022 service date is a 2021 forecast, not the later reported actual; July 2023 materials report January 25, 2023 revenue service and closeout. [annual_report_narrative_2021#p088_c0003] [meeting_doc_115231#p011_c0010]

The page aliases merge core ESA/GCM, support-project briefings, passenger-experience closeout, and fire-suppression contract work. This page treats these as related phases/items, not one identical scope. [meeting_doc_100311#p003_c0017] [meeting_doc_100311#p003_c0018] [meeting_doc_147196#p018_c0008]

Overview

These sources describe East Side Access Support Projects primarily as a Long Island Rail Road Committee work-plan update, not as a standalone scope description. In the 2023 work plan, the item appears in November 2023 alongside Winter Trackwork Programs [meeting_doc_102721#p002_c0007] [meeting_doc_102721#p002_c0008]. The detailed entry says the Committee would be briefed on the status of the East Side Access Support Projects [meeting_doc_102721#p005_c0008] [meeting_doc_102721#p005_c0009] [meeting_doc_102721#p005_c0010].

Later 2023 work-plan versions repeat the same November status-briefing language [meeting_doc_111736#p004_c0021] [meeting_doc_111736#p004_c0022] [meeting_doc_111736#p004_c0023] [meeting_doc_124186#p001_c0008] [meeting_doc_124186#p001_c0009] [meeting_doc_124186#p004_c0001] [meeting_doc_124186#p004_c0002]. A November 2024 work plan again pairs an East Side Access Support Projects Update with Winter Trackwork Programs, and again describes the support-project item as a committee status briefing [meeting_doc_160086#p002_c0015] [meeting_doc_160086#p002_c0016] [meeting_doc_160086#p006_c0007] [meeting_doc_160086#p006_c0008] [meeting_doc_160086#p006_c0009].

Related Trackwork Context

Related trackwork context appears nearby but should be read carefully. Summer Track Work Programs are described as schedule adjustments supporting various trackwork programs, Main Line Second Track construction, and East Side Access Readiness projects [meeting_doc_102721#p004_c0015] [meeting_doc_124186#p005_c0025] [meeting_doc_124186#p005_c0026]. The November 2023 Winter Trackwork Programs entry instead identifies switch installations near Jamaica, switch maintenance near Valley Stream, and rail maintenance on the Wreck Lead Bridge [meeting_doc_124186#p004_c0003] [meeting_doc_124186#p004_c0004].

Caveats

The support-project sources do not identify specific subprojects, budget, locations, metrics, or outcomes; they only state that the Committee would receive a status briefing.

East Side Access "Readiness" appears in related trackwork language, but the cited blocks do not explicitly say those readiness projects are the same thing as the "Support Projects Update."

The November 2024 Winter Trackwork block mentions West Side Yard switch installations, but its OCR text repeats part of the phrase "plan to temporarily adjust schedules" [meeting_doc_160086#p006_c0011].
